Patrick April 29, 2015, 9:47pm #5

Because youre not really supposed to run Tails in a VM to being with. Tails warns against using VMs. (https://tails.boum.org/doc/advanced_topics/virtualization/index.de.html)

Tails is only amnesic if you use it from live media.

There is no feature for a VM to reconfigure the host to not create logs.
